REVERSIONERS - YOU'RE ABSOLUTELY RIGHT
KILL THEM. HERE'S WHY:
The Narrative Headaches You Identified:
1. Timeline Paradoxes:

"I'll just reverse that bad thing!"

"Wait, if it never happened, why do you remember it?"

"Does everyone remember both timelines?"

"Which timeline is 'real'?"

[Infinite questions, no good answers]
2. Stakes Elimination:

Character dies → Reversioner undoes it
Disaster happens → Reversioner fixes it
Bad choices → Reversioner resets

[Nothing has consequences]
[Why care about anything?]
3. Plot Convenience:

Stuck in corner? Reversioner!
Made mistake? Reversioner!
Need reset? Reversioner!

[Deus ex machina on demand]
[Readers smell contrivance]
4. Power Creep:

If Reversioners exist, why haven't they:
- Prevented Shattering?
- Saved everyone who died?
- Fixed all disasters?
- Made world perfect?

[Their existence raises questions]
[Questions have no good answers]

Your Other Four Powers:
Quantumancers:

Manipulate FUTURE (collapse possibilities ahead)
Active, present-focused
Consequences going forward
Forward-looking
Readers:

Read PRESENT (understand now)
Passive observation
No timeline manipulation
Present-focused
Echoes:

View PAST (see what was)
Passive observation
No changes, just viewing
Backward-looking (safe)
Nullwraiths:

OUTSIDE quantum (invisible to it)
Defensive/blocking
Negation, not creation
Orthogonal to timeline
Reversioners:

Edit PAST (change what was)
Active manipulation
Timeline alteration
Backward-looking (dangerous)

Defensive/Protective

Nullwraith = void
Anchor = fixation
Complementary not redundant

Protect important locations
Prevent Quantumancer attacks
Stabilize chaotic quantum areas
Mobile "safe zones"
Defensive support

WEAVERS - HEALTH NOT TRUTH
PERFECT DISTINCTION:
THE DIFFERENCE:
Readers vs. Weavers:
READERS:

Care about TRUTH
"What IS real?"
"What is Prime?"
"What is actually happening?"
Objective reality
Truth-seekers
WEAVERS:

Care about HEALTH
"What connections are strong?"
"What threads are damaged?"
"What is complete vs. broken?"
Relational wellness
Health-seekers
Key Difference:

Reader looking at relationship:
"They say they're friends. Are they actually?"
[Truth/falsehood]

Weaver looking at same relationship:
"Their connection is frayed here, strong here."
"Doesn't matter if it's 'true' friendship."
"What matters: is it healthy? Complete?"
[Health/damage]
WHAT WEAVERS SEE:
Not Truth, But Condition:
The Threads:

Strong threads (healthy connections)
Weak threads (damaged connections)
Fraying threads (deteriorating)
Severed threads (broken bonds)
Structural integrity, not truth
They Don't Care:

"Is this a real friendship?"
[Reader question - truth]

They DO Care:
"Is this connection healthy?"
[Weaver question - wellness]
Example:

Two people claim to be enemies.

Reader: "They're lying. They actually care about 
each other deeply."
[Detects falsehood, reveals truth]

Weaver: "Their thread is twisted but strong. 
It's damaged by external pressure but the core 
connection is whole. They could reconcile easily 
if the pressure released."
[Assesses health, suggests repair path]

[Different information entirely]
THE ASSESSMENT FRAMEWORK:
What Weavers Evaluate:
Connection Strength:

Robust (survives stress)
Fragile (breaks under pressure)
Resilient (heals after damage)
Brittle (shatters completely)
Structural integrity
Connection Health:

Nourishing (both parties benefit)
Parasitic (one drains other)
Toxic (damages both parties)
Healing (actively repairing)
Wellness assessment
Connection Completeness:

Whole (fully formed)
Partial (one-sided)
Fragmented (inconsistent)
Incomplete (developing)
Wholeness evaluation
They DON'T See:

Whether connection is "true"
Whether feelings are "real"
Whether claims are honest
That's Reader territory
PRACTICAL DIFFERENCES:
In Action:
Scenario: Suspected Traitor

Reader Approach:

"Is this person actually loyal?"
[Yes/No answer]
[Truth revealed]
Weaver Approach:

"This person's connections to team are fraying badly."
"Their thread to the enemy is strengthening."
"The bond isn't severed yet, but it's damaged."
[Health assessment]
[Trajectory shown]
[But not WHY - that's not their domain]
Different Intel:

Reader: "They're a traitor" (truth)
Weaver: "Their loyalty bond is dying" (health)
Both useful
Neither complete without context
Complementary information
SCENARIO: LOISA & GRAYSON
After Burmallosca:
Reader Would See:

"They claim it was just operational necessity."
"Is that true?"

[Examines their actual feelings]
"Yes, that's true. No romantic feelings."
[Truth confirmed]
Weaver Sees:

[Looking at their connection]

"Their thread is incredibly strong."
"The incident didn't damage it - it reinforced it."
"Some stress marks here and here, but healing."
"Healthy bond, complete trust, no fractures."
[Health assessment]

[Doesn't care if it's 'true' it was just operational]
[Cares that their connection is STRONG and HEALTHY]
Loisa as Weaver:

[Looking at her own connection to Grayson]

"We're solid. Our thread is one of the strongest 
I've ever seen."

[When Elsbeth enters picture]

"New thread forming. Strong from the start."
"It's not weakening ours. Different type of bond."
"His capacity for connection is large."

[Sees health, not competition]
[Understands structural integrity]
SCENARIO: HARA'S GROWTH
Weaver Perspective:
Early Journey:

Weaver looking at Hara:

"Her self-connection is severely damaged."
"Thread to her own competence is almost severed."
"Connections to others are one-sided - she gives, 
doesn't receive."
[Unhealthy structure]
After Gabby Intervenes:

"Self-connection strengthening."
"Competence thread reweaving."
"Bonds to others becoming reciprocal."
[Health improving]
By Journey's End:

"Self-connection is whole."
"She's structurally sound now."
[Complete healing]
Weaver Doesn't Care:

Whether her confidence is "real" (Reader question)
Just that her structure is healthy
Health, not truth
GUIDING QUANTUMANCERS:
The Repair Work:
Quantumancer Without Weaver:

"I can collapse this possibility."

[Collapses it]

[Doesn't see: broke three connections, weakened 
two others, left one person structurally unsound]

[Consequences invisible]
Quantumancer With Weaver:

"I can collapse this possibility."

Weaver: "That collapse will sever this connection 
and damage these two."

"What if I collapse this way instead?"

Weaver: "That strengthens this thread and completes 
this partial bond. Much healthier."

[Guided manipulation]
[Health-conscious choices]
Not About Truth:

Weaver doesn't say:
"That collapse creates false outcome."
[Truth-based objection]

Weaver says:
"That collapse creates damaged structure."
[Health-based objection]

[Different framework entirely]
THE MEDICAL METAPHOR:
Perfect Analogy:
Reader = Diagnostician:

"What IS wrong?"
"Is this really cancer or misdiagnosis?"
"What is the TRUTH of the condition?"
Truth-seeker
Weaver = Surgeon/Therapist:

"How damaged is this tissue?"
"Can this connection heal?"
"What intervention creates best health?"
Health-optimizer
Quantumancer = Surgeon's Hands:

Can cut, repair, alter
But needs Weaver's guidance
"Where do I cut for best healing?"
Power guided by wisdom
LOISA'S INTELLIGENCE WORK:
As Weaver:
Mapping Networks:

Not asking: "Who is REALLY in charge?"
[Truth question - Reader's domain]

Asking: "Where are the strong connections?"
"Which relationships are load-bearing?"
"What thread, if severed, collapses network?"
[Health/Structure questions - Weaver's domain]
Strategic Planning:

Not: "What's the TRUE threat?"
[Reader question]

But: "Which enemy connections are weakest?"
"Where can we break bonds most easily?"
"What alliance can we strengthen?"
[Health-based strategy]
Team Management:

Not: "Who's REALLY loyal?"
[Reader question]

But: "Whose connections to team are fraying?"
"Who needs relationship strengthening?"
"Where are the stress fractures?"
[Health-based leadership]

FINAL ANSWER:
Yes. Keep this distinction.

Weavers assess HEALTH and COMPLETENESS, not truth.

They see:

Strong vs. weak
Damaged vs. whole
Healthy vs. toxic
Complete vs. fragmented
They don't see:

True vs. false
Real vs. fake
Honest vs. lying
That's Reader territory. Completely different domain.

THE HORROR STORY EXAMPLES:
What People Believe:
The Collapse Child:

"In my grandfather's time, a boy in the village could 
make things happen just by wishing. He wanted his 
bully to fall, and the boy's legs snapped. He wanted 
food, and it appeared. They say he wanted his father 
to stop beating his mother, and his father's heart 
just... stopped.

The village elders said he was cursed. They locked him 
in his house and burned it down. Better one cursed 
child than a whole cursed village."

[Quantumancer killed by mob]
[Became cautionary tale]
[Now used to justify more murders]
The Truth-Seer:

"There was a woman who always knew when you lied. 
Always. She'd look at you and just KNOW. People said 
she could see your soul. She exposed the mayor's 
affair, the merchant's cheating, the priest's theft.

Then people got scared. 'What does she know about ME?' 
they thought. One night, she disappeared. They found 
her in the river, stones in her pockets. Everyone 
knew. No one spoke of it."

[Reader killed by community]
[Truth was dangerous]
[Murder became unspoken agreement]
The Ghost Watcher:

"My grandmother told me about a girl who saw things 
that weren't there. She'd stare at empty space and 
talk about people from long ago. She'd tell stories 
about events no one alive remembered.

They said she was touched by spirits. That the dead 
spoke through her. The Church took her away 'for 
examination.' She never came back. My grandmother 
said it was mercy."

[Echo captured by Church]
[Became ghost story]
[Used to frighten children]
The Invisible One:

"There's stories about people you can't quite remember. 
You talk to them, but later you forget their face. You 
look at them and your eyes slide away. Some say they're 
cursed to be unseen. Some say they're already dead, 
just walking around.

Most people avoid them. Bad luck to acknowledge what 
shouldn't be noticed."

[Nullwraith, but superstition wrong]
[Actually just quantum-invisible]
[Feared without understanding]
THE CYCLE OF FEAR:
How Stories Perpetuate Hunting:
Step 1: Event Happens

Quantum-gifted child manifests ability.
Something impossible occurs.
Witnesses see it.
[Actual event]
Step 2: Story Forms

"Did you hear what happened?"
Details added, embellished.
Fears projected onto story.
Becomes more frightening in retelling.
[Mythology building]
Step 3: Story Spreads

Told to children as warning.
Passed to other villages.
Grows more elaborate.
Original truth buried.
[Cultural transmission]
Step 4: Story Justifies Violence

New quantum-gifted appears.
Someone remembers the stories.
"We know what happens if we don't act."
Mob forms, justified by history.
[Fear becomes weapon]
Step 5: New Story Created

"We had to kill them before they killed us."
Event becomes another horror story.
Cycle continues.
[Self-perpetuating terror]

"He's MY best friend"
Fear of losing priority
Recognizes feelings, adapts
Makes peace with new dynamic
All three become comfortable
PART 3: THE SWAT SEQUENCE
Three-Beat Structure:
First Swat (Gabby → Calder):

Calder going off on Hara (too harsh, typical veteran behavior)
Hara melting (mouse personality, can't defend herself)
Gabby stands up, swats Calder (NCIS Gibbs-slap instinct)
Does "I'm watching you" fingers (American gesture)
Calder confused (doesn't know Earth references), backs off
Realizes he was too harsh
Instinctive protection, Earth behavior slip
Loisa's Response:

Recognizes Earth behavior immediately
Coaches Gabby privately: "Something from where you come from" (vague, no specifics)
Earth culture concealment protocol
Protects her from exposure
Second Swat (Elsbeth → Calder):

Calder forgotten, does it again to Hara
Elsbeth learned context from Gabby
MUCH harder swat
Private lecture follows
Calder actually learns, apologizes to Hara
Authority enforcement, proper correction
Third Swat (Both → Calder):

Weeks later
Hara now stands firm (grown confident)
Calder performs exaggerated caricature (self-aware, playful)
Eyes glittering, watching for them
Gabby and Elsbeth simultaneous swat (playful)
Everyone laughs
Inside joke, group bonding, growth shown
Character Arcs Shown:

Gabby: Fierce loyalty, acts on instinct, Earth slips
Hara: Mouse → confident (can stand up for herself)
Calder: Obtuse → self-aware (learns through correction)
Elsbeth: Authority with humor
Group: Conflict → correction → bond

PART 6: QUANTUM-ADJACENT ABILITIES SYSTEM
The Five Powers:
1. QUANTUMANCERS (Active/Future)

Collapse possibilities into reality
Manipulate probability
See "ghost images" of potential futures
Choose which becomes real
More probable = easier, less probable = harder
Cost: Quantum haze drives them insane
Status: Functionally extinct (hunted as children, can't hide use)
Example: Chance Hodgkins (disembodied soul, only "free" one)
2. READERS (Passive/Present/Truth)

Read current Prime (reality as it IS)
See truth/falsehood
Understand actual state
Ground others in reality
Can't manipulate, just observe
Example: Alyzandra (Chance's anchor, long dead)
Status: Rare, hiding (seem insightful)
3. WEAVERS (Passive/Present/Health)

See quantum connections between people/things
Assess health/damage of threads
Care about HEALTH not truth
Strong vs. weak, whole vs. broken, healthy vs. toxic
Guide Quantumancers to "healthy" collapses
Enable repair of quantum fabric
Can't manipulate alone, need Quantumancer
Example: Possibly Loisa (hidden)
Status: Rare, hiding (seem like good therapists/strategists)
4. ECHOES (Passive/Past)

View past events (rewind quantum like VCR)
Experience historical record
NOT changing it, just viewing
Can witness what actually happened
Example: Gabby (possibly only known one)
Status: Very rare, endangered
5. NULLWRAITHS (Outside/Negation)

Invisible to quantum perception
Project field that's outside quantum
Can't be detected by quantum abilities
Block/suppress nearby quantum powers
Completely passive (most don't know what they are)
Example: Solon (Church's known asset)
Status: Possibly thousands (unknown), only Solon confirmed
Key Distinctions:
Readers vs. Weavers:

Reader: "Is this connection TRUE?" (truth/falsehood)
Weaver: "Is this connection HEALTHY?" (strong/weak, whole/broken)
Different questions, different information, both valuable
Echoes vs. Reversioners (REJECTED):

Originally had "Reversioners" who could EDIT quantum past
REJECTED due to: timeline paradoxes, stakes elimination, narrative headaches, contrivance
Echo = view past (safe, passive, no paradoxes)
Much better for story
Power + Guidance = Repair:

Quantumancer = power without wisdom (dangerous)
Weaver = wisdom without power (limited)
Together = can repair quantum damage healthily
Apostasy mission: not just resistance, but healing post-Shattering damage
PART 7: PERSECUTION OF QUANTUM-GIFTED
Three Threats:
1. Church of Malachor (Institutional):

Official doctrine: quantum-gifted caused Shattering
Must be eliminated (religious duty)
Organized: Inquisitors, informant networks, priests report unusual events
Systematic investigation and capture
2. Locquodian Order (Unknown - INFORMATION GAP):

Mentioned as second hunting organization
You said we discussed them before
I don't have this information
CRITICAL MISSING ELEMENT
3. Superstitious Population (Mob Justice):

Folk horror stories passed down generations
Embellished over time, grain of truth + mountain of fear
Cultural mythology: quantum-gifted = cursed, bring disasters, possessed
Vigilante violence, torches and pitchforks, no trial
Self-perpetuating cycle: event → story → spread → justifies next murder
Folk Tales Examples:

The Collapse Child (Quantumancer killed by mob, became cautionary tale)
The Truth-Seer (Reader murdered for knowing too much)
The Ghost Watcher (Echo captured by Church, "mercy")
The Invisible One (Nullwraith feared without understanding)
Status: NOT Extinct, HUNTED:
Still Being Born:

Genetic lines intact
Natural manifestation continues
Normal birth rates
But Aggressively Hunted:

Active powers (Quantumancers) = immediately visible = caught young
Passive powers (others) = concealable = survival possible
Visibility = Danger:

PASSIVE (Safe if careful):
- Nullwraiths: Completely passive, most don't know what they are (thousands alive?)
- Readers: Seem insightful, plausibly deniable (hundreds hiding)
- Echoes: Internal viewing, looks like daydreaming (dozens, endangered)
- Weavers: If just viewing, safe; if manipulating, riskier (dozens?)

ACTIVE (Extremely dangerous):
- Quantumancers: Can't hide use, reality changes visibly (5-10 alive, hiding in terror)
Population Estimates:

Nullwraiths: Thousands (unknown to themselves and others)
Readers: Hundreds (hiding, seem insightful)
Echoes: Dozens (very rare, endangered)
Weavers: Dozens (uncertain)
Quantumancers: 5-10 (functionally extinct, survive through never using power)
Survival Strategy:

Hide abilities completely
Never reveal to anyone
Pass as normal
Any slip = death from Church, Locquodians, or mob
PART 8: EARTH CULTURE CONCEALMENT
The Protocol:
Academy Training:

Keep Earth references inside Academy walls
Mask behaviors, gestures, idioms
Blend into Iolinus culture
Operational security essential
Why:

Earthers = Apostasy connection (Church knows)
Cultural slips = identification
Identification = death sentence
No Earth "tourists" on Iolinus
Gabby's Challenges:

New, young, American (impulsive, direct)
Training incomplete
Instincts Earth-based (NCIS, pop culture)
Slips occasionally
Loisa's Coaching:

Recognizes Earth behavior immediately (fellow Earther)
"Something from where you come from" (vague, no specifics)
Never say "Earth," no TV shows, no specific references
Protect through ambiguity
Examples:

Elsbeth accepts without prying (respects boundaries)

Blinding pain in brain

Hiking in mountains

Should have died

Discovered he could stop aging
Became immortal

Reader (saw current Prime, grounded him)
His anchor to reality
Argued with her constantly (even after death)

Witnessed Thohalla desert crossing
Over 50% died (no water preparation)
Zeta turned tragedy into religious ritual
Week-long mortification, ends with salt water
Modern Thohalla still practice (moderated version)
Blame victims: "those who drank from sea when faith flagged"
Theological abuse commemorated

Nala manipulated him and other Quantumancers
Tried to destroy Godstone
Succeeded in shattering it (not destroying)
His body destroyed in attempt
Soul survived (quantum nature)
Still exists as disembodied Quantumancer

Mad, wants to complete Shattering

Needs body to finish quantum work
Major antagonist for later books
"By Chance" Document:

His confession/justification
Written before Shattering attempt
Thousands of years before Gabby's era
Found later, read in present
Title = wordplay (by Chance + by chance/probability)
Modern language justified: Malachor's translation gift + addressing future readers

PART 15: PROSE STYLE DISCUSSION
Modern Language in Fantasy:
Your Approach:

Contemporary narrator voice (Chance writing for future)
"Freaking" and modern profanity
Casual syntax
No fake medievalisms
Why It Works:

Chance is 10,000 years old, writing in HIS present
Translation gift justifies modern comprehension
He explicitly says he's making it readable
Emotional authenticity > period accuracy
Avoids Aubrey-Maturin problem (cognitive load from archaic language)
You Were Right:

"I don't want to bog readers down with unnatural words"
Archaic prose = slog (you love Aubrey-Maturin but acknowledge the problem)
Story > authenticity
Comprehension > immersion
Reader experience prioritized
Comparison:

Following Gene Wolfe, Susanna Clarke, Nabokov (literary fiction technique in fantasy)
NOT traditional Tolkien elevated prose
Different goals: connection over immersion
Self-selecting audience (literary SFF readers)
Would Be Contrived:

Your instinct about Reversioners (time-travel editing past)
Recognizing when complexity serves plot not story
Trusting simplicity over gimmicks
